function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1179') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.1179!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('README.md')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: README.md');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('README.md')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): README.md');
	} else if (sha1_file('README.md') != 'f7313487ed6e7d6cf9c0c9ba73c23ba8c60cfd87') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): README.md');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('README.md', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of README.md');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('README.md') !== 'f7313487ed6e7d6cf9c0c9ba73c23ba8c60cfd87') {
		if (@sha1_file('README.md') !== '893e369b33b17b21bb5588458feb033ecb65bdd1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: README.md');
			$tmp = pathinfo('README.md');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('README.md')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('README.md', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('README.md') !== 'f7313487ed6e7d6cf9c0c9ba73c23ba8c60cfd87') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): README.md');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '13b2270ae041530498c99ad4be8c5147ce8a20a2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '13b2270ae041530498c99ad4be8c5147ce8a20a2') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '505f27fee7416a5fdc91882b306e442c50e73466') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '13b2270ae041530498c99ad4be8c5147ce8a20a2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}
